This is a relatively well-known old hotel in Shenyang. It still retains the high-end taste and is prosperous. I have a soft spot for old hotels. It is unmatched by newly opened hotels. Parking is also very convenient. The front desk is on the 10th floor. Check-in is very convenient and can be done in five minutes. The room is opposite the Hun River. The view is great. I like it. Looking at the scenery in this place, the floor arrangement is very reasonable, and fruit desserts are arranged after check-in. It is really a surprise, and the price-performance ratio is very high. If I remember correctly, I called the guest relations director Evian, who was very enthusiastic and took the initiative to help me with parking access knowing that I was driving. I had a problem, and I found something missing in the hotel. She was the first to help me deal with it. She was very enthusiastic and would be my first choice next time I come to Shenyang.
